\subsection{Initialization Phase: Dual Problem Solving}
New Objective in primal was changed to : \[ \max\ \sum_{j=1}^{5}\ - x_j \] 
Primal variable $x_j$ corresponds to dual variable $y_j$ for $j = 1,\ldots,12$
